expand_urban_regions_category = {
	urbanize_state_POL = {
		icon = GFX_decision_hol_attract_foreign_investors
		state_target = yes
		#on_map_mode = map_only
		target_array = POL.owned_states
		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = 150
		cost = 175
		days_re_enable = 50
		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 10
		}
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_core_of = ROOT
				OR = {
					has_state_category = rural
					has_state_category = town
					has_state_category = large_town
					has_state_category = city
					has_state_category = large_city
					has_state_category = metropolis
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			POL = {
				has_completed_focus = POL_finish_land_reform
			}
		}
		available = {
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 10
			#ROOT = {
			#	owns_state = FROM
			#}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							has_state_category = wasteland
						}
					}
					set_state_category = pastoral
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							has_state_category = tiny_island
						}
					}
					set_state_category = pastoral
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							has_state_category = pastoral
						}
					}
					set_state_category = rural
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							has_state_category = tiny_island
						}
					}
					set_state_category = small_island
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							has_state_category = small_island
						}
					}
					set_state_category = rural
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							has_state_category = rural
						}
					}
					set_state_category = town
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							has_state_category = town
						}
					}
					set_state_category = large_town
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							has_state_category = large_town
						}
					}
					set_state_category = city
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							has_state_category = city
						}
					}
					set_state_category = large_city
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							has_state_category = large_city
						}
					}
					set_state_category = metropolis
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							has_state_category = metropolis
						}
					}
					set_state_category = megalopolis
				}
			}
		}	
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
		}
	}
}

	topple_the_tyrants = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_reorganize_irregulars

						}
					}

					capital_scope = {

				add = 40
			}
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { FROM.num_of_factories > ROOT.num_of_factories }
				add = -40
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50

					strength_ratio = {
						tag = FROM 
						ratio > 1.5 
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -50
				ROOT = {
					strength_ratio = {
						tag = FROM 
						ratio < 1.5 
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_capitulated = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				ROOT = {
					has_wargoal_against = FROM
				}
